<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">невѣжа</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nevěža</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*nevěďa</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ignorant person lt; ignorance</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*ne-</i> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*věďa</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*věděti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to know</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невежда.html>неве́жда</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nevéžda</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невежа.html>неве́жа</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nevéža</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невежа.html>неве́жи</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невежа.html>неве́жи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невежа.html>неве́ж</a></b>)

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:везение.html>везе́ние</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vezénije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невезение.html>невезе́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nevezénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невезение.html>невезе́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невезение.html>невезе́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невезение.html>невезе́ний</a></b>)

***невероятный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:невероятный.html>невероя́тный</a> (3025)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невероятный.html>невероя́тный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">neverojátnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>improbable</li>
<li>unbelievable</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Ему́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:выписать.html>вы́писали</a> <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;"><a href = vnd.unilang:невероятный.html>невероя́тный</a></span> <a href = vnd.unilang:гонорар.html>гонора́р</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рубль.html>рубля́х</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:превышающий.html>превыша́ющий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:гонорар.html>гонора́р</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всего́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:оркестр.html>орке́стра</a>. </span> <span class="example-fullblock"></li>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black"><a href = vnd.unilang:дикий.html>Ди́кие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кабан.html>кабаны́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:поросенок.html>порося́тами</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:поднять.html>подняли</a> <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;"><a href = vnd.unilang:невероятный.html>невероя́тный</a></span> <a href = vnd.unilang:визг.html>визг</a>. </span></li>
</ul></li>

</ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:верующий.html>ве́рующий</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vérujuščij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неверующий.html>неве́рующий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nevérujuščij</span>)

<ol><li>unbelieving, disbelieving, nonbelieving</li>
<li>irreligious, faithless</li>
<li>pagan</li>

</p>
<ol><li>atheist, disbeliever, nonbeliever, unbeliever, pagan, infidel</li></ol>

<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black"><a href = vnd.unilang:только.html>То́лько</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>одному́</a> <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;"><a href = vnd.unilang:неверующий.html>неве́рующему</a></span> <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>слова́м</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>мои́м</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:недоступный.html>недосту́пному</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мысль.html>мы́слям</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:высокий.html>высо́ким</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:позволительный.html>позволи́тельно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сделать.html>сделать</a>. </span>} <span class="example-fullblock"></li>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black">― Для чего вы, <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">неверующий</span> в истины света и не <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">видящий</span> света, для чего вы пришли сюда, чего хотите вы от нас? </span> <span style="display: none"><span style="display: none"></span></li>
</ul></li>


<li>не признающий существования Бога <span class="example-fullblock"><ul>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black">И он, он — тоже ослеплённый и <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">неверующий</span>, — он тоже сейчас услышит, он тоже уверует, да, да! </span> <span class="example-fullblock"></li>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black">Он, <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">неверующий</span>, стал молиться и в ту минуту, как молился, верил. </span> <span style="display: none"></span></li>
</ul></li>


<li><span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="<a href = vnd.unilang:выступать.html>выступа́ет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:роль.html>ро́ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>существи́тельного</a>">субстантивир.</span> тот, кто ни во что не верит <span class="example-fullblock"><ul>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black">В противоположность отцам, дети представляют собой собрание <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">неверующих</span>. — Вы не верите ни во что… даже? — вопрошает Базарова один из Кирсановых. — Даже, — отвечает Базаров, вовсе не заботясь о том, что он делает этот ответ в доме Кирсановых и что, по всем правилам гостеприимства, гость обязан говорить хозяевам лишь приятные и угодные вещи. </span> <span style="display: none"><span style="display: none"></span></li>
</ul></li>


<li><span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="<a href = vnd.unilang:выступать.html>выступа́ет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:роль.html>ро́ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>существи́тельного</a>">субстантивир.</span> тот, кто не верит в Бога <span class="example-fullblock"><ul>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black"> — Скажи, о чём ты молишься, Вера? — О <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">неверующих</span>… — тихо сказала она. </span> <span class="example-fullblock"></li>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black"> — Ты, <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">неверующий</span>, молчи, молчи, пока Бог постучится к тебе в сердце. </span> <span class="example-fullblock"></li>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black">И на сердце ни печали, ни досады, ни заботы нет; тут и <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">неверующий</span> в бога поверует. </span> <span style="display: none"></span></li>
</ul></li>

</ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:невеста.html>невеста</a> (2704)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*nevěsta</i>. Probably from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">not</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ведать.html>ве́дать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">védatʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to know</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, indicating a strict hands-off relationship.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невеста.html>неве́ста</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nevésta</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невеста.html>неве́сты</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невеста.html>неве́сты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невеста.html>неве́ст</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>fiancée, bride</li>
<li>marriageable girl</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:молодой.html>молода́я</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">molodája</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:новобрачный.html>новобра́чная</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">novobráčnaja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***невестка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:невестка.html>неве́стка</a> (12076)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невеста.html>неве́ста</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nevésta</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belarusian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Belarusian language">Belarusian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be">няве́стка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">njavjéstka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невестка.html>неве́стка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nevéstka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невестка.html>неве́стки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невестка.html>неве́стки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невестка.html>неве́сток</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>a woman’s daughter-in-law <i>(husband’s daughter-in-law is <a href = vnd.unilang:сноха.html>сноха́</a>)</i></li>
<li>sister-in-law <i>(the wife of one’s brother or brother-in-law)</i></li></ol>

<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взирать.html>взира́я</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vzirája</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, present adverbial participle of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взирать.html>взира́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vzirátʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to look, to gaze</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; compare <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">regardless</i>, literally "without looking".

***невзлюбить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:невзлюбить.html>невзлюби́ть</a> (20761)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:любить.html>люби́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ljubítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:невиданный.html>неви́данный</a> (7002)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:видать.html>ви́данный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vídannyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, past passive participle of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:видать.html>вида́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vidátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невидимка.html>невиди́мка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nevidímka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невидимка.html>невиди́мки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невидимка.html>невиди́мки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невидимка.html>невиди́мок</a></b>)

***невидимый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:невидимый.html>неви́димый</a> (2437)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*nevidimъ</i>, equivalent to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:видеть.html>ви́димый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vídimyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невидимый.html>неви́димый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nevídimyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)неви́димее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)неви́димей</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:самый.html>са́мый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:невидимый.html>неви́димый</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>invisible</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:невиновность.html>невино́вность</a> (14700)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невиновный.html>невино́вный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nevinóvnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:невкусный.html>невку́сный</a> (23572)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вкусный.html>вку́сный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vkúsnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невкусный.html>невку́сный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nevkúsnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)невку́снее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)невку́сней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>tasteless, insipid, unappetizing</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> ironic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> unpleasant</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Per Zaliznyak, the comparative <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">невку́снее</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nevkúsneje</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is rare and awkward.</li></ul>

<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вкусный.html>вку́сно</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vkúsno</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">v</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">мог-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mog-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-оту́</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-otú</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Predicative">Predicative</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невмоготу.html>невмоготу́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nevmogotú</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> it is unbearable, intolerable, unendurable (to, for)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:невод.html>не́вод</a> (22807)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невод.html>не́вод</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">névod</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невод.html>не́вода</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невод.html>невода́</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невод.html>не́воды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невод.html>неводо́в</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невод.html>не́водов</a></b>)
